Here lies Kanye "Ye" West 
    (1977-2022)

      “We got to stop dissing the 
      Nazis all the time”

  (Hours after the interview, 
  Ye tweeted an image of a 
  swastika intertwined with 
  a Star of David. “YE24 
        LOVE EVERYONE 
        #LOVESPEECH,” 
        he wrote.)

      Ye's hate speech has 
      cost him. In October, 
      Adidas ended a deal with 
      Ye - divesting him of 
      his billionaire status.

        (1990-2022)
    
        Found guilty of rape by a 
        Beijing court and sentenced 
        to 13 years in prison.

          that he [Wu] selects 
          concubines among 
          international students."

Here lies Ned Fulmer
          (1987-2022)
      
              Woman claims she caught 
              fired Try Guys star Ned 
              Fulmer cheating in May
      
          News broke in September 
          that Ned had an affair 
          with Try Guys producer 
          Alex Herring.
      
            "Family should have 
            always been my priority, 
            but I lost focus and had 
            a consensual workplace 
            relationship..."

Here lies Ezra Miller
        (1992-2022)
    
        Parents obtained a 
        protective order against 
        Miller for allegedly physically 
        and emotionally abusing their 
        18-year-old daughter.
    
      A mother and her child, 
      now 12, were granted a 
      temporary harassment 
      prevention order 
      against Miller.

    "I now understand that I am 
    suffering complex mental 
    health issues and have 
    begun ongoing treatment."

(5)

Here lies Balenciaga (Demna)
        (1919-2022)
    
  The fashion house came under 
  fire at the end of 2022 for 
  two different campaigns, one 
  of which featured children 
  holding teddy bears that 
  were outfitted in 
  bondage-style leather outfits.
    
            The backlash against 
            the images was swift, 
            with the hashtag 
            #cancelBalenciaga 
            trending across Twitter 
            and TikTok and many 
            accusing the brand and 
            its creative director, 
            Demna, of condoning 
            pedophilia and 
            child exploitation.

(6)

Here lies Clarence Thomas
          (1948-2022)
      
    Supreme Court Justice 
    Clarence Thomas has accepted 
    secret luxury trips from 
    Republican megadonor Harlan 
    Crow for more than two decades, 
    ProPublica reported.
      
The investigation offers more 
fuel for Thomas’ critics, who 
say his refusal to recuse himself 
from cases touching on issues 
related to his wife’s political 
work in conservative circles 
— including her involvement in 
schemes to overturn the 2020 
election — poses a conflict 
of interest.

Here lies Rex Orange County
          (1998-2022)
      
The 24-year-old British 
musician, whose real name 
is Alex O’Connor, was 
slapped with claims of 
sexual abuse by a woman 
who alleges he assaulted 
her in London on six 
separate occasions.
    
    The singer’s accuser alleges he 
    sexually assaulted her twice in 
    West London on June 1, and an 
    additional four times the 
  following day, including once 
  in a taxi and the other three 
  times in his Notting Hill home, 
  The Sun reports.

Here lies Andrew Tate
          (1986-2022)
      
    Tate, a 36-year-old known 
    for his misogynistic views, 
    was detained in Bucharest 
    (Dec 2022) on charges of rape, 
    human trafficking and running 
    an organized crime ring. Tate's 
    brother and two Romanian 
    citizens were included in 
    the initial rounds of arrests.

Tate, a professional 
kickboxer who has 
resided in Romania 
since 2017, was 
previously banned 
from various social 
media platforms for 
expressing misogynistic 
views and hate speech.

          (1979-2022)

  claimed that Levine "manipulated"
